data-reactid="95"></div></div></div><div id="main-content" data-reactid="96"><article class="page livePage layout-live_event" data-reactid="97"><div class="molecule liveHeader" data-reactid="98"><h1 data-reactid="99">WWE SmackDown: Live Updates, Reaction and Analysis for February 14</h1><!-- react-empty: 100 --><div class="atom liveLocation" data-reactid="101"><span class="datetime" data-reactid="102">1:00am UTC Feb 15, 2017</span><span class="location" data-reactid="103">Anaheim, California</span></div><span class="atom authorInfo" data-reactid="104"><a href="/users/64083" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-reactid="105"><span class="name" data-reactid="106">The Doctor Chris Mueller</span></a><span class="title" data-reactid="107"></span></span><p class="description" data-reactid="108">Welcome to Bleacher Report&#x27;s live coverage for WWE SmackDown on February 14. The blue brand looks a lot different following Elimination Chamber. Bray Wyatt is now the WWE champion, and Naomi is the women&#x27;s champion. Tuesday&#x27;s show will see John Cena face Wyatt in a rematch for the WWE Championship. With no more pay-per-views before WrestleMania for SmackDown, we can expect management to start to build more storylines for the biggest event of the year.
